Statement</h1>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  vc_custom_1452627900792\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h3 style=\"text-align: center;
